def _resolve_jawal_batch_paths(batch_id):
    normalized = batch_id.replace("jawal-", "")
    batch_dir = ROOT / "batches" / f"jawal-{normalized}"

    try:
        import discover
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[warn] Could not import discover.py: {e}", flush=True)
        fallback_raw = batch_dir / "raw"
        if batch_dir.exists() and fallback_raw.exists():
            print(f"[warn] Using legacy hardcoded fallback paths because discover.py import failed for {normalized}", flush=True)
            return batch_dir, fallback_raw, None
        return None, None, f"discover.py import failed: {e}"

    discovery_roots = [
        batch_dir / "raw",
        ROOT / "archive" / f"raw-{normalized}",
        ROOT / "raw",
    ]
    old_raw = getattr(discover, "RAW", None)
    try:
        for raw_root in discovery_roots:
            if not raw_root.exists():
                continue
            discover.RAW = raw_root
            try:
                cfg = discover.discover_jawal()
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"[warn] discover.py found no Jawal batch data under {raw_root}: {e}", flush=True)
                continue
            invoice_path = cfg.invoice_xlsx.resolve(strict=False)
            if normalized not in str(invoice_path):
                print(f"[warn] discover.py ignored {invoice_path}; expected batch {normalized}", flush=True)
                continue
            return batch_dir, raw_root, None
    finally:
        if old_raw is not None:
            discover.RAW = old_raw

    return None, None, f"discover.py returned no paths for batch {normalized}"

    return jsonify({"status": "ok"})

@app.route('/process', methods=['GET'])
        proc4 = subprocess.Popen(cmd4, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT, text=True, bufsize=1)
        for line in iter(proc4.stdout.readline, ''):
            yield f"data: {line.strip()}\n\n"
        proc4.wait()
        
        if proc4.returncode != 0:
            yield f"data: [API] Stage 4 (Excel Injection) failed with code {proc4.returncode}\n\n"
            yield "data: [END]\n\n"
            return

        # STAGE 4.5: Rebuild portal review JSON
        yield f"data: [API] >> STAGE 4.5: Rebuilding portal review JSON from v30 spreadsheet...\n\n"

        for line in iter(proc45.stdout.readline, ''):
            yield f"data: {line.strip()}\n\n"
        proc45.wait()

        if proc45.returncode != 0:
            yield f"data: [API] Stage 4.5 (Portal Review JSON) failed with code {proc45.returncode}\n\n"
            yield "data: [END]\n\n"

            h["_agent_method"] = h.pop("_agent_method_orig")

    print(f"[out] {out_xlsx.name} (v30 pass complete)", flush=True)

    # ── stage 4.4: v30 — regenerate text label columns for LLM-resolved rows ────
    # Root cause fix: after LLM resolves numeric combo codes (account/CC/agency),
    # the text label columns (GL name, Cost Name, Contribution/DIV label, Solution Name,
    # Agency Name, GL Description) retained cascade values derived from the pre-filled
    # wrong employee. This makes the human-readable output misleading even when the
    # numeric Distribution Combination is correct.
    # Fix: for every LLM-resolved row, parse the written combo and regenerate all text
    # labels via code_name_lookup before stage 4.5 appends trailing zeros.
    _LLM_METHODS = {
        # normalised names written to xlsx
        "llm_agent", "hybrid_overlay", "cluster_unified",
        # original v16 names (restored after write_v15_12_xlsx)
        "v16_master_shortcut", "v16_sponsorship_master",
        "v16_llm_agent", "v16_llm_agent_pc_override",
        "v16_hybrid_overlay",
        # v30 overlay methods that also update combo codes
        "v26_nts_pc_overlay", "v26_emp_registration",
        "v25_personal_contribution",
    }
    # The code_name_lookup requires a file with an INDEX worksheet (lookup tables).
    # Prefer the current batch, then fall back to the configurable reference batch.
    _ref_batch_id = LOOKUP_REFERENCE_BATCH
    _ref_batch_dir = ROOT / "batches" / f"jawal-{_ref_batch_id}"
    _ref_fixture_key = _ref_batch_id.lower().replace("j26-", "j")
    _ref_xlsx = None
    for _candidate in [
        batch_dir / "output" / f"Spreadsheet-{batch_id}-FILLED-validation.xlsx",
        batch_dir / f"{batch_id}.xlsx",
        _ref_batch_dir / "output" / f"Spreadsheet-{_ref_batch_id}-FILLED-validation.xlsx",
        _ref_batch_dir / f"{_ref_batch_id}.xlsx",
        ROOT / "qc" / "fixtures" / f"golden-{_ref_fixture_key}" / f"jawal-{_ref_batch_id.lower()}-resolved.xlsx",
    ]:
        if _candidate.exists():
            _ref_xlsx = _candidate
            break
    try:
        if _ref_xlsx and _ref_xlsx.exists():
            from code_name_lookup import get_lookup
            _lookup = get_lookup(str(_ref_xlsx))
            _wb27 = openpyxl.load_workbook(out_xlsx)
            _ws27 = _wb27.active
            _h27 = {str(c.value).strip(): i + 1 for i, c in enumerate(_ws27[hdr_row]) if c.value}
            _combo_col = next((v for k, v in _h27.items() if "distribution combination" in k.lower()), None)
            _label_updated = 0
            for _hyb in hybrid_rows:
                _meth = _hyb.get("_agent_method", "")
                if _meth not in _LLM_METHODS:
                    continue
                _ri = _hyb["_row_idx"]
                # Get the combo that was written to Excel
                if _combo_col:
                    _combo = str(_ws27.cell(row=_ri, column=_combo_col).value or "")
                else:
                    _pa = lambda v, w: str(v or "").strip().zfill(w) if str(v or "").strip().isdigit() else str(v or "").strip() or "0" * w
                    _combo = (
                        f"03-20100-{_pa(_hyb.get('account'),8)}-{_pa(_hyb.get('cost_center'),6)}"
                        f"-{_pa(_hyb.get('div'),3)}-{_pa(_hyb.get('solution'),5)}-{_pa(_hyb.get('agency'),5)}"
                        f"-00000-00-000000"
                    )
                _exp = _lookup.expand_combo(_combo)
                # Write individual label columns
                for _col_name, _exp_key in [
                    ("GL",            "GL"),
                    ("Cost Name",     "Cost Name"),
                    ("Contribution",  "Contribution"),
                    ("Solution Name", "Solution Name"),
                    ("Agency Name",   "Agency Name"),
                ]:
                    if _col_name in _h27:
                        _v = (_exp.get(_exp_key) or "").strip()
                        if _v and _v != "#N/A":
                            _ws27.cell(row=_ri, column=_h27[_col_name], value=_v)
                # Rebuild GL Description (5-part; stage 4.5 adds trailing zeros)
                if "GL Description" in _h27:
                    def _c(v):
                        s = (v or "").strip()
                        return s if s and s != "#N/A" else "\u2014"
                    _gl_desc = " \u00b7 ".join([
                        _c(_exp.get("GL", "")),
                        _c(_exp.get("Cost Name", "")),
                        _c(_exp.get("Contribution", "")),
                        _c(_exp.get("Solution Name", "")),
                        _c(_exp.get("Agency Name", "")),
                    ])
                    _ws27.cell(row=_ri, column=_h27["GL Description"], value=_gl_desc)
                _label_updated += 1
            _wb27.save(str(out_xlsx))
            print(f"[v30-labels] {_label_updated} rows: text labels regenerated from resolved combo", flush=True)
        else:
            print(f"[v30-labels] WARN: reference xlsx not found for {batch_id} or {_ref_batch_id} — skipping label regeneration", flush=True)
    except Exception as _lbl_err:
        import traceback
        print(f"[v30-labels] ERROR: {_lbl_err}\n{traceback.format_exc()}", flush=True)

    # ── stage 4.4: v30 — Force rewrite cascade locations from Manpower ───────────
    try:
        _wb_loc = openpyxl.load_workbook(out_xlsx)
        _ws_loc = _wb_loc.active
        
        # Load manpower quickly
        import pandas as pd

+def _resolve_jawal_batch_paths(batch_id):
+    normalized = batch_id.replace("jawal-", "")
+    batch_dir = ROOT / "batches" / f"jawal-{normalized}"
+
+    try:
+        import discover
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"[warn] Could not import discover.py: {e}", flush=True)
+        fallback_raw = batch_dir / "raw"
+        if batch_dir.exists() and fallback_raw.exists():
+            print(f"[warn] Using legacy hardcoded fallback paths because discover.py import failed for {normalized}", flush=True)
+            return batch_dir, fallback_raw, None
+        return None, None, f"discover.py import failed: {e}"
+
+    discovery_roots = [
+        batch_dir / "raw",
+        ROOT / "archive" / f"raw-{normalized}",
+        ROOT / "raw",
+    ]
+    old_raw = getattr(discover, "RAW", None)
+    try:
+        for raw_root in discovery_roots:
+            if not raw_root.exists():
+                continue
+            discover.RAW = raw_root
+            try:
+                cfg = discover.discover_jawal()
+            except Exception as e:
+                print(f"[warn] discover.py found no Jawal batch data under {raw_root}: {e}", flush=True)
+                continue
+            invoice_path = cfg.invoice_xlsx.resolve(strict=False)
+            if normalized not in str(invoice_path):
+                print(f"[warn] discover.py ignored {invoice_path}; expected batch {normalized}", flush=True)
+                continue
+            return batch_dir, raw_root, None
+    finally:
+        if old_raw is not None:
+            discover.RAW = old_raw
+

+def _resolve_jawal_batch_paths(batch_id):
+    normalized = batch_id.replace("jawal-", "")
+    batch_dir = ROOT / "batches" / f"jawal-{normalized}"
+
+    try:
+        import discover
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"[warn] Could not import discover.py: {e}", flush=True)
+        fallback_raw = batch_dir / "raw"
+        if batch_dir.exists() and fallback_raw.exists():
+            print(f"[warn] Using legacy hardcoded fallback paths because discover.py import failed for {normalized}", flush=True)
+            return batch_dir, fallback_raw, None
+        return None, None, f"discover.py import failed: {e}"
+
+    discovery_roots = [
+        batch_dir / "raw",
+        ROOT / "archive" / f"raw-{normalized}",
+        ROOT / "raw",
+    ]
+    old_raw = getattr(discover, "RAW", None)
+    try:
+        for raw_root in discovery_roots:
+            if not raw_root.exists():
+                continue
+            discover.RAW = raw_root
+            try:
+                cfg = discover.discover_jawal()
+            except Exception as e:
+                print(f"[warn] discover.py found no Jawal batch data under {raw_root}: {e}", flush=True)
+                continue
+            invoice_path = cfg.invoice_xlsx.resolve(strict=False)
+            if normalized not in str(invoice_path):
+                print(f"[warn] discover.py ignored {invoice_path}; expected batch {normalized}", flush=True)
+                continue
+            return batch_dir, raw_root, None
+    finally:
+        if old_raw is not None:
+            discover.RAW = old_raw
+
+    return None, None, f"discover.py returned no paths for batch {normalized}"
+

+def _resolve_jawal_batch_paths(batch_id):
+    normalized = batch_id.replace("jawal-", "")
+    batch_dir = ROOT / "batches" / f"jawal-{normalized}"
+
+    try:
+        import discover
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"[warn] Could not import discover.py: {e}", flush=True)
+        fallback_raw = batch_dir / "raw"
+        if batch_dir.exists() and fallback_raw.exists():
+            print(f"[warn] Using legacy hardcoded fallback paths because discover.py import failed for {normalized}", flush=True)
+            return batch_dir, fallback_raw, None
+        return None, None, f"discover.py import failed: {e}"
+
+    discovery_roots = [
+        batch_dir / "raw",
+        ROOT / "archive" / f"raw-{normalized}",
+        ROOT / "raw",
+    ]
+    old_raw = getattr(discover, "RAW", None)
+    try:
+        for raw_root in discovery_roots:
+            if not raw_root.exists():
+                continue
+            discover.RAW = raw_root
+            try:
+                cfg = discover.discover_jawal()
+            except Exception as e:
+                print(f"[warn] discover.py found no Jawal batch data under {raw_root}: {e}", flush=True)
+                continue
+            invoice_path = cfg.invoice_xlsx.resolve(strict=False)
+            if normalized not in str(invoice_path):
+                print(f"[warn] discover.py ignored {invoice_path}; expected batch {normalized}", flush=True)
+                continue
+            return batch_dir, raw_root, None
+    finally:
+        if old_raw is not None:
+            discover.RAW = old_raw
+
+    return None, None, f"discover.py returned no paths for batch {normalized}"
+

     return jsonify({"status": "ok"})

+def _resolve_jawal_batch_paths(batch_id):
+    normalized = batch_id.replace("jawal-", "")
+    batch_dir = ROOT / "batches" / f"jawal-{normalized}"
+
+    try:
+        import discover
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"[warn] Could not import discover.py: {e}", flush=True)
+        fallback_raw = batch_dir / "raw"
+        if batch_dir.exists() and fallback_raw.exists():
+            print(f"[warn] Using legacy hardcoded fallback paths because discover.py import failed for {normalized}", flush=True)
+            return batch_dir, fallback_raw, None
+        return None, None, f"discover.py import failed: {e}"
+
+    discovery_roots = [
+        batch_dir / "raw",
+        ROOT / "archive" / f"raw-{normalized}",
+        ROOT / "raw",
+    ]
+    old_raw = getattr(discover, "RAW", None)
+    try:
+        for raw_root in discovery_roots:
+            if not raw_root.exists():
+                continue
+            discover.RAW = raw_root
+            try:
+                cfg = discover.discover_jawal()
+            except Exception as e:
+                print(f"[warn] discover.py found no Jawal batch data under {raw_root}: {e}", flush=True)
+                continue
+            invoice_path = cfg.invoice_xlsx.resolve(strict=False)
+            if normalized not in str(invoice_path):
+                print(f"[warn] discover.py ignored {invoice_path}; expected batch {normalized}", flush=True)
+                continue
+            return batch_dir, raw_root, None
+    finally:
+        if old_raw is not None:
+            discover.RAW = old_raw
+
+    return None, None, f"discover.py returned no paths for batch {normalized}"
+

+def _resolve_jawal_batch_paths(batch_id):
+    normalized = batch_id.replace("jawal-", "")
+    batch_dir = ROOT / "batches" / f"jawal-{normalized}"
+
+    try:
+        import discover
+    except Exception as e:
+        print(f"[warn] Could not import discover.py: {e}", flush=True)
+        fallback_raw = batch_dir / "raw"
+        if batch_dir.exists() and fallback_raw.exists():
+            print(f"[warn] Using legacy hardcoded fallback paths because discover.py import failed for {normalized}", flush=True)
+            return batch_dir, fallback_raw, None
+        return None, None, f"discover.py import failed: {e}"
+
+    discovery_roots = [
+        batch_dir / "raw",
+        ROOT / "archive" / f"raw-{normalized}",
+        ROOT / "raw",
+    ]
+    old_raw = getattr(discover, "RAW", None)
+    try:
+        for raw_root in discovery_roots:
+            if not raw_root.exists():
+                continue
+            discover.RAW = raw_root
+            try:
+                cfg = discover.discover_jawal()
+            except Exception as e:
+                print(f"[warn] discover.py found no Jawal batch data under {raw_root}: {e}", flush=True)
+                continue
+            invoice_path = cfg.invoice_xlsx.resolve(strict=False)
+            if normalized not in str(invoice_path):
+                print(f"[warn] discover.py ignored {invoice_path}; expected batch {normalized}", flush=True)
+                continue
+            return batch_dir, raw_root, None
+    finally:
+        if old_raw is not None:
+            discover.RAW = old_raw
+
+    return None, None, f"discover.py returned no paths for batch {normalized}"
+
